<date>1629339670126<//date><Rating>5< /Rating>< review>
I have been bringing my dog, Oliver, to Smart Parke for about six weeks. Oliver is a 2 1/2  YO  rescue who led a very challenging life before I was fortunate enough to bring him into my home about five months ago.

I cannot say enough good things about Smart Parke and its amazing staff.  The facility is first class, from entry , to the dogs' diverse and entertaining areas to departure.  Beyond that, without exception, everyone I have encountered or worked with at SP has been friendly, caring, helpful, patient and  knowledgeable in all interactions with me and, more importantly, with Oliver.  When he and I arrive and depart, we are treated as friends and family and not just customers.  And, during his stays, Oliver is in dog heaven.

Smart Parke and, most importantly, its amazing staff, has helped make Oliver an even happier, more special dog than he was already before we found this special place.

If you want to enhance your dog's life (and your own as part of the process) bring them to Smart Parke under whatever flexible   (and very affordable) program that works for you and your pup.

Sincerely,
Marc S<//review>

Excellent quality of care and supervision for our dog Apollo who had his first overnight stay. The camera access to the main day camp areas are a huge plus and gave us a lot of reassurance about leaving him alone for the first time. We watched how the staff were extremely attentive to the dogs and clean up their accidents ASAP. Plenty of space for the density of dogs at any given time. I‚Äôd say there was a max of about 30 or so dogs in the main day camp area, and the indoor and outdoor spaces is plenty of space for that number of dogs. Despite the large number of dogs, I didn‚Äôt see any serious scuffles between dogs. If any dogs did play a bit rowdy, the staff interrupted them right away. That was extremely reassuring knowing my dog is safe and happy. Also, booking over phone or text is super easy, which was an awesome benefit for us since we had to reschedule very last minute a couple times.

My only critique is the camera in the sleeping quarters. It was pointed mainly at the wall, making up probably about 3/4ths of the entire camera view. So we didn‚Äôt really get the chance to see how our dog was doing. This is probably a super simple fix for them, so hopefully they will take care of that soon. I‚Äôm still giving 5 stars for the overall quality, price, and staff at this facility, because I doubt any other facilities can compare.</review>

{'time': 1625702327545, 'text': "We are sorry and surprised to hear that you had such a negative experience. Our overnight accommodations do include a half day of camp, 24 hours web cameras so you can monitor your pet, maid service every day, house cuisine, staff on site 24/7 so pets are never left unattended and a complimentary bath on their last day. The vast majority of facilities do not offer all of these services as part of the fee.\n\nFor the half day of camp that is included with every dog's stay, we split that time up so each dog gets a few hours in the morning and a few hours in the late afternoon. Many facilities offer a half day of camp in one block and then the dogs have to wait until the next day to go back to camp. We feel it is better for the dogs to split it up. Clients do have the choice to upgrade their pet to have a full day of Day Camp for a nominal fee. We also offer all sorts of upgrades so you can tailor your pets stay (Peanut Butter Kongs, Frozen Yogurt, one-on-one Cuddle time, etc.).\n\nWe offer our house cuisine at no additional charge. If a pet is on a personal diet,  we have a kitchen just for the pets that includes refrigerators, freezers and a microwave. We charge $3 per day for pets to have their own personal diets. If a pet is not eating we reach out to the owner to get permission to use enticement (such as wet food or treats). We do not charge for that service.\n\nIn Day Camp, we do not allow toys because pets can become possessive and resource guard items. This can cause conflicts between the dogs which we do not want. Our staff's goal is to safely monitor the dogs in Day Camp so they can safely engage in play with one another and not to offer personalized one-on-one attention to each individual pet in Day Camp. This can cause conflicts with dogs as well since they can become possessive over staff. We do recommend if you would like more personalized attention for your pet that you can add on a one-on-one Cuddle time.\n\nIn an off leash Day Camp environment, dogs do play with their mouths and bodies. It is very common for there to be minor scrapes and scratches - just like with kids going to kindergarten. If there ever is an incident that is more serious, we thoroughly evaluate the dog and report any wounds immediately to the owner. We would have liked to speak with you directly regarding your concerns but could not find you in our system. Please call our facility and ask to speak wo one of the Managers directly so we can speak directly. We wish you and your pet the best wherever you chose to go in the future."}</Resp>

Kusco seemed to enjoy his time at Smart Parke.  Of course, maybe the best way to tell is to bring him back and see his reaction to going back inside!
My feedback would be that your operation seems very professional and smoothly-run, and your staff seemed to interact very well with the dogs.  One suggestion, though: you may want to improve the very end of the evaluation process in terms of formalizing the feedback to the owner.  When we picked up Kusco, we were told that if we wanted feedback on Kusco's visit, we should ask the person who brought him to the front, who unfortunately had already left by then (i.e., gone into the back with the dogs).
Fortunately, the person we asked about getting feedback was, herself, able to give feedback, so it worked out.  I would suggest a very small form with 3 to 4 checkboxes indicating how the dog interacted with the other fur-babies.

<userid>106223895657420090443</userid><Name>iTrishelle Daly<//Name><Time>1619365328417</Time><Rating>3< /Rating>< review>
SmartPark caught my eye for boarding and daycare because of their outdoor space and ability to view the dogs in their rooms while boarding. As it turns out both of these things are very limited. When I first took my dog for daycare they were able to go back and forth inside and outside. That only happened that one time now the gate is closed and they are only allowed outside for short periods a few times a day. The cameras in their rooms for sleeping only look at the bed the ceiling and the walls. You cannot see the entire room. You don't know if they are walking around on their own filth, have water in their bowl, panting, pacing, or relaxed and peaceful. If you have more than one dog sharing the room often times you cannot even tell if the second dog is in there.
Every member of the team I have encountered has been pleasant . I do question some of their level of expertise. The team members in the yard often just sit there, they do not move around much.  The dogs are often left in the yard (inside and outside) by them self with no supervision. It is typically for a very short period of time, but it can be concerning.
I feel with more training and better staffing this will ultimately be a great day care. I will continue to take my dogs for short periods of time but will continue to watch and monitor very close.< /review>

<rate>5</rate>< text>
This place is a hidden gem. The food served by this restaurant is what Indians generally eat at home, but prepared with highest quality ingredients. Other good Indian restaurants serve what Indian restaurants offer in India, not what people generally eat in their everyday life.
I see that some people have complained about the prices, but I think the prices are reasonable given that this is a specialty restaurant,  even among the Indian ones. I have also seen someone mention in their review that khichdi is poor man's food in India. Clearly the person has no idea about Indian culture. Khichdi is an ubiquitous comfort food which is often served to people who are sick. Khichdi is also offered to the gods during worshipping rituals. Like most Indian vegetarian food, khichdi can be cheap in India and therefore affordable to most.

We are Indian and we love this food.</text>

< review>
HelloTech experience was horrible.

I bought a wall mount from Walmart.  I paid Walmart to have the wall mount attached to the wall in the bedroom.  Walmart contracted HelloTech to do the job.

I showed the HelloTech tech the wall mount I had purchased and showed him where to mount it in the bedroom.  I also told him that the TV in the kitchen will go to the bedroom and a new TV will go in the kitchen.  He did NOT tell us that was not what he was going to do.  Instead he just attached the new TV to the existing wall mount in the kitchen.

Then he said he needed to go to Home Depot to get some tools to install the wall mount in the bedroom.  He never came back.  I found out later he had marked the job completed.  He never installed the wall mount to the bedroom wall - which is what I had paid for.  And he lied to us about going to Home Depot to get tools.< /review>

I was looking for used tires to use temporarily until I had my suspension repaired next week. A young man came out and told me they have 245/45/20 that would fit the front of my car, I told them I'm not sure if that would fit. They guaranteed it would.
Here's where it gets pretty scary
They told me it would be 160 dollars.
I've never paid more than 35 to 40 dollars for a used tire.
I asked to see what tires they were planing on selling me.
They rolled them out and I was offended. The front tires were around 3 or 4/32nds of tread left The rear was offensive. It probably had 1 or 2/32nds of tread left.
I told them I am not okay with these tires. They rolled out new ones that had slightly more tread.
But then preceded to tell me these cost more valued at 170!
At this point I'm blown away. They started telling me I had to pay disposal fees if I use my bank card but if I pay cash I would not have to pay them.
Unbelievable.
I've never paid disposal fees on any used tire. Ever.
They changed their price after I started to walk away to 140 even. I said fine because I had to leave to Vegas that night and my time was running thin.

"If it ain't broke, don't fix it" seems to be a fitting motto for the SB Chicken Ranch. This casual local walk-up Mexican style BBQ joint has been serving from the same simple menu for decades, and yet, like In and Out Burger, people still come in droves to get their favorite dish. The service is quick, the food is plentiful, and the salsa bar is always free.< /Text>
